PREFACE
One of the most remarkable rediscoverers of the profound
teachings of the Guru Rimpoche Padmasambhava was Rig -'dzin 'Ja ':
Ishon- snying.no (1585-1650) of Kong.po. This guru is also known
variously as Gter-ston Las - phro-gling-pa and Sngags-'chang Hum .
nag-me-'bar. His monastic ordination name was Ngag.dbang-chos.
rgyal-dbang-po. but this is seldom encountered in his numerous
revelations and prolific writings.
This volume of the Smanrisis Shesrig Spend zod series contains
'Ja'-tshon-shying po's gter-mia concerned with Avalokiteſvara
(Mahakarunika). These teachings are especially interesting when
viewed in connection with the Ma ni bka 'bum ,
'Ja -tshon-snying.pa was born at Waru Gnam -tshal in Kong
po . His chief gurus included the Drugpa Kargyudpa masters,
Brug-chen Dpag-bsam -dbang po (1593- 1641), Lha-rtse-ba Ngag.
dbang-bzang po (1546-1616), and Mi-pham -bkra - shis-blo-gros, and
the great Dwags-po Zhabs-drung Nor-bu -brgyan -pa ( 1688- 1833).
Unlike most gfer-ston , 'Ja -Eshon-snying-po remained a monk through
out his life . His most famous germa rediscoveries were the Yang
zab dan ntchog spyi 'dus, the Riabhag yid bzhin mor bu, and the Zhi
khro nges dont saying po. The masters upon whom had bestowed these
extraordinarily efficacious teachings included the greatest Kargyudpa
and Nyingmapa masters of the age.
